self.window_seconds\n        timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n\n        # Check if limit exceeded\n        if len(timestamps) >= self.requests_per_window:\n            return HttpResponse(\n                f'Rate limit exceeded. IP: {client_ip}',\n                status=403\n            )\n\n        # Record this request\n        timestamps.append(current_time)\n        return None\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract the client IP address from the request.\n        \"\"\"\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get('HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR')\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            ip = x_forwarded_for.split(',')[0].strip()\n            return ip\n        return request.META.get('REMOTE_ADDR', '0.0.0.0')\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self, current_time):\n        \"\"\"\n        Remove IP entries that have no recent requests.\n        \"\"\"\n        window_start = current_time - self.window_seconds\n        ips_to_delete = []\n\n        for ip, timestamps in self.ip_timestamps.items():\n            # Keep only recent timestamps\n            timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n            # If no timestamps left, mark for deletion\n            if not timestamps:\n                ips_to_delete.append(ip)\n\n        # Delete empty entries\n        for ip in ips_to_delete:\n            del self.ip_timestamps[ip]\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1008,"cache_read_input_tokens":54196,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1008},"output_tokens":7,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"224f16a3-9a7e-4845-8a30-df46f29ccd0a","uuid":"c62d0b50-68fb-4be7-a7f8-390788d1d5e2"}

self.window_seconds\n        timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n\n        # Check if limit exceeded\n        if len(timestamps) >= self.requests_per_window:\n            return HttpResponse(\n                f'Rate limit exceeded. IP: {client_ip}',\n                status=403\n            )\n\n        # Record this request\n        timestamps.append(current_time)\n        return None\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract the client IP address from the request.\n        \"\"\"\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get('HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR')\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            ip = x_forwarded_for.split(',')[0].strip()\n            return ip\n        return request.META.get('REMOTE_ADDR', '0.0.0.0')\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self, current_time):\n        \"\"\"\n        Remove IP entries that have no recent requests.\n        \"\"\"\n        window_start = current_time - self.window_seconds\n        ips_to_delete = []\n\n        for ip, timestamps in self.ip_timestamps.items():\n            # Keep only recent timestamps\n            timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n            # If no timestamps left, mark for deletion\n            if not timestamps:\n                ips_to_delete.append(ip)\n\n        # Delete empty entries\n        for ip in ips_to_delete:\n            del self.ip_timestamps[ip]\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

self.window_seconds\n        timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n\n        # Check if limit exceeded\n        if len(timestamps) >= self.requests_per_window:\n            return HttpResponse(\n                f'Rate limit exceeded. IP: {client_ip}',\n                status=403\n            )\n\n        # Record this request\n        timestamps.append(current_time)\n        return None\n\n    def get_client_ip(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Extract the client IP address from the request.\n        \"\"\"\n        x_forwarded_for = request.META.get('HTTP_X_FORWARDED_FOR')\n        if x_forwarded_for:\n            ip = x_forwarded_for.split(',')[0].strip()\n            return ip\n        return request.META.get('REMOTE_ADDR', '0.0.0.0')\n\n    def cleanup_expired_entries(self, current_time):\n        \"\"\"\n        Remove IP entries that have no recent requests.\n        \"\"\"\n        window_start = current_time - self.window_seconds\n        ips_to_delete = []\n\n        for ip, timestamps in self.ip_timestamps.items():\n            # Keep only recent timestamps\n            timestamps[:] = [ts for ts in timestamps if ts > window_start]\n            # If no timestamps left, mark for deletion\n            if not timestamps:\n                ips_to_delete.append(ip)\n\n        # Delete empty entries\n        for ip in ips_to_delete:\n            del self.ip_timestamps[ip]\n","numLines":83,"startLine":1,"totalLines":83}}}
